SELECT `o0`.`OrderId`, `o`.`OrderDetailId`, `o0`.`OrderDate`, `s`.`Username` AS `CustomerName`, `s`.`ShopperRegId` AS `ShopperId`, `p`.`product_id` AS `ProductId`, `p`.`product_name` AS `ProductName`, `o`.`Quantity`, CAST(`o`.`Quantity` AS decimal(65,30)) * `o`.`Price` AS `Amount`, CASE
    WHEN `p0`.`PaymentId` IS NOT NULL THEN `p0`.`PaymentStatus`
    ELSE 'Unpaid'
END AS `PaymentStatus`, `p0`.`PaymentId` AS `TransactionId`, `s`.`Address`, `s`.`Town`, `s`.`City`, `s`.`State`, `s`.`Country`, CASE
    WHEN `s0`.`ShippingDetailId` IS NOT NULL THEN `s0`.`Shipping_type`
    ELSE 'Standard'
END AS `DeliveryType`, CASE
    WHEN `s0`.`ShippingDetailId` IS NOT NULL THEN `s0`.`ShippingStatus`
    ELSE 'Not Shipped'
END AS `ShippingStatus`
FROM `OrderDetails` AS `o`
INNER JOIN `Orders` AS `o0` ON `o`.`OrderId` = `o0`.`OrderId`
INNER JOIN `ShopperRegisters` AS `s` ON `o0`.`ShopperRegId` = `s`.`ShopperRegId`
